<span class="td-post-author-name"><a href="https://timurexpress.co/author/redaktur/">Redaksi</a> <span>-</span> </span>                <span class="td-post-date"><time class="entry-date updated td-module-date" datetime="2025-12-08T21:54:24+08:00">8 Desember 2025</time></span>                <span class="td-module-comments"><a href="https://timurexpress.co/bupati-bolmong-tinjau-langsung-pembangunan-enam-titik-jalan-usaha-tani/#respond">0</a></span></div><div class="td-excerpt">
BOLMONG, timurexpress.co - Bupati Bolaang Mongondow (Bolmong), Yusra Alhabsyi, meninjau pembangunan enam jalan usaha tani yang di anggarkan melalui APBD Perubahan Kabupaten Bolmong Tahun...</div></div></div><div class="td-block-span6"><div class="td_module_2 td_module_wrap td-animation-stack"><div class="td-module-image"><div class="td-module-thumb"><a href="https://timurexpress.co/bupati-bolmong-rakor-bersama-ratusan-sangadi-bolmong/" rel="bookmark" class="td-image-wrap " title="Bupati Bolmong Rakor Bersama Ratusan Sangadi Bolmong"><img data-lazyloaded="1" src="data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyB4bWxucz0iaHR0cDovL3d3dy53My5vcmcvMjAwMC9zdmciIHdpZHRoPSIzMjQiIGhlaWdodD0iMTYwIiB2aWV3Qm94PSIwIDAgMzI0IDE2MCI+PHJlY3Qgd2lkdGg9IjEwMCUiIGhlaWdodD0iMTAwJSIgZmlsbD0iI2NmZDRkYiIvPjwvc3ZnPg==" loading="lazy" decoding="async" width="324" height="160" class="entry-thumb" data-src="https://timurexpress.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/12/xRakor-Penyelenggaraan-Pemerintah-Desa-324x160.jpg.pagespeed.ic.pPqymYODRM.jpg" data-srcset="https://timurexpress.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/12/xRakor-Penyelenggaraan-Pemerintah-Desa-324x160.jpg.pagespeed.ic.pPqymYODRM.jpg 324w, https://timurexpress.co/wp-content/uploads/2025/12/xRakor-Penyelenggaraan-Pemerintah-Desa-533x261.jpg.pagespeed.ic.FqAtIpViQR.jpg 533w" data-sizes="auto, (max-width: 324px) 100vw, 324px" alt="Bupati Bolmong Yusra Alhabsyi, Rakor Penyelenggaraan Pemerintah Desa bersama camat, para Sangadi wilayah Kabupaten Bolaang Mongondow, di Balai Desa Tungoi I, Kecamatan Lolayan, Bolmong, 4 Desember 2025.
